<content>
1: package com.trulyfreeocr.pipeline;
2: 
3: import java.awt.Graphics2D;
4: import java.awt.Rectangle;
5: import java.awt.image.BufferedImage;
6: import java.io.BufferedReader;
7: import java.io.File;
8: import java.io.IOException;
9: import java.io.InputStreamReader;
10: import java.util.ArrayList;
11: import java.util.List;
12: 
13: import javax.imageio.ImageIO;
14: 
15: import com.trulyfreeocr.model.PageResult;
16: import com.trulyfreeocr.model.TextBlock;
17: 
18: /**
19:  * OCR engine that delegates to the Tesseract CLI via subprocess.
20:  *
21:  * Tess4J's JNA binding was originally planned, but lept4j's
22:  * Leptonica version requires symbols not present in the system's
23:  * liblept.so.5.  Running tesseract as a subprocess (with TSV output)
24:  * avoids this native-library version mismatch entirely and is more
25:  * portable across Linux distributions.
26:  *
27:  * Tesseract output format: TSV (tab-separated values) with columns:
28:  *   level, page_num, block_num, par_num, line_num, word_num,
29:  *   left, top, width, height, conf, text
30:  *
31:  * CLI flags used:
32:  *   -l eng    — English language model
33:  *   --psm 1   — Automatic page segmentation with OSD
34:  *   tsv       — Output format: TSV (word-level bounding boxes)
35:  *
36:  * The output PageResult always reports pageNumber=1 because each
37:  * call processes exactly one BufferedImage.
38:  */
39: public class OCREngine {
40: 
41:     private final File tessdataDir;
42:     private final String tesseractPath;
43:     private final String language;
44:     private final String psm;
45: 
46:     public OCREngine() {
47:         this("tessdata", "native/linux/tesseract", "eng", "1");
48:     }
49: 
50:     public OCREngine(String tessdataDir, String tesseractPath, String language, String psm) {
51:         this.tesseractPath = tesseractPath;
52:         this.language = language;
53:         this.psm = psm;
54: 
55:         if (tessdataDir != null && !tessdataDir.isEmpty()) {
56:             this.tessdataDir = new File(tessdataDir);
57:         } else {
58:             String env = System.getenv("TESSDATA_PREFIX");
59:             if (env != null && !env.isEmpty()) {
60:                 this.tessdataDir = new File(env);
61:             } else {
62:                 this.tessdataDir = new File("/usr/share/tesseract-ocr/5/tessdata");
63:             }
64:         }
65:     }
66: 
67:     public PageResult ocr(BufferedImage image) throws IOException {
68:         int width = image.getWidth();
69:         int height = image.getHeight();
70: 
71:         // Convert to grayscale — Tesseract processes 8-bit gray ~100x faster than 24-bit RGB
72:         if (image.getType() != BufferedImage.TYPE_BYTE_GRAY) {
73:             BufferedImage gray = new BufferedImage(width, height, BufferedImage.TYPE_BYTE_GRAY);
74:             Graphics2D g = gray.createGraphics();
75:             g.drawImage(image, 0, 0, null);
76:             g.dispose();
77:             image = gray;
78:         }
79: 
80:         // Write image to temp file
81:         File tempPng = File.createTempFile("tfocr-", ".png");
82:         tempPng.deleteOnExit();
83:         ImageIO.write(image, "png", tempPng);
84: 
85:         try {
86:             // Run tesseract with TSV output for word-level bounding boxes
87:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
88:             ProcessBuilder pb = new ProcessBuilder(
89:                     tesseractPath,
90:                     tempPng.getAbsolutePath(),
91:                     prefix,
92:                     "-l", language,
93:                     "--psm", psm,
94:                     "tsv"
95:             );
96:             pb.environment().put("TESSDATA_PREFIX", tessdataDir.getAbsolutePath());
97:             pb.redirectErrorStream(true);
98: 
99:             Process process = pb.start();
100:             try (BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(
101:                     new InputStreamReader(process.getInputStream()))) {
102:                 // Read and discard stdout (status messages go here)
103:                 while (reader.readLine() != null) { }
104:             }
105:             boolean exited = process.waitFor(30, java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit.SECONDS);
106:             if (!exited) {
107:                 process.destroyForcibly();
108:                 throw new IOException("Tesseract timed out after 30 seconds");
109:             }
110:             int exitCode = process.exitValue();
111:             if (exitCode != 0) {
112:                 throw new IOException("Tesseract exited with code " + exitCode);
113:             }
114: 
115:             // Parse TSV output
116:             File tsvFile = new File(prefix + ".tsv");
117:             if (!tsvFile.exists()) {
118:                 return new PageResult(1, width, height, List.of());
119:             }
120: 
121:             List<TextBlock> blocks = parseTsv(tsvFile);
122:             return new PageResult(1, width, height, blocks);
123: 
124:         } catch (InterruptedException e) {
125:             Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
126:             throw new IOException("Tesseract was interrupted", e);
127:         } finally {
128:             // Cleanup temp files
129:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
130:             for (String ext : new String[]{".png", ".tsv"}) {
131:                 File f = new File(prefix + ext);
132:                 if (f.exists()) f.delete();
133:             }
134:         }
135:     }
136: 
137:     private List<TextBlock> parseTsv(File tsv) throws IOException {
138:         List<TextBlock> blocks = new ArrayList<>();
139:         try (BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new java.io.FileReader(tsv))) {
140:             String header = reader.readLine(); // skip header
141:             if (header == null) return blocks;
142: 
143:             String line;
144:             while ((line = reader.readLine()) != null) {
145:                 if (line.trim().isEmpty()) continue;
146:                 String[] parts = line.split("\t");
147:                 // TSV columns: level, page_num, block_num, par_num, line_num, word_num,
148:                 //              left, top, width, height, conf, text
149:                 if (parts.length < 12) continue;
150: 
151:                 String level = parts[0];
152:                 String text = parts[11].trim();
153:                 if (!"5".equals(level) || text.isEmpty()) continue; // word level only
154: 
155:                 try {
156:                     int left = Integer.parseInt(parts[6]);
157:                     int top = Integer.parseInt(parts[7]);
158:                     int w = Integer.parseInt(parts[8]);
159:                     int h = Integer.parseInt(parts[9]);
160:                     double conf = Double.parseDouble(parts[10]);
161: 
162:                     blocks.add(new TextBlock(text, new Rectangle(left, top, w, h), conf));
163:                 } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
164:                     // skip malformed lines
165:                 }
166:             }
167:         }
168:         return blocks;
169:     }
170: }

(End of file - total 170 lines)

1: package com.trulyfreeocr.util;
2: 
3: import java.io.File;
4: 
5: /**
6:  * Cross-platform detection utilities.
7:  *
8:  * Provides consistent enum values for OS and CPU architecture,
9:  * and resolves the project JDK location via the TFOCR_JAVA_HOME
10:  * environment variable (falling back to the running JVM's java.home).
11:  *
12:  * OS detection is based on the os.name system property:
13:  *   "win" in any case   → Os.WINDOWS
14:  *   "mac" in any case   → Os.MAC
15:  *   anything else       → Os.LINUX
16:  *
17:  * Architecture detection is based on os.arch:
18:  *   "aarch64" or "arm64" → Arch.AARCH64
19:  *   anything else         → Arch.X64
20:  */
21: public class PlatformUtils {
22: 
23:     public enum Os { WINDOWS, LINUX, MAC }
24: 
25:     public enum Arch { X64, AARCH64 }
26: 
27:     public static Os detectOs() {
28:         String raw = System.getProperty("os.name").toLowerCase();
29:         if (raw.contains("win")) return Os.WINDOWS;
30:         if (raw.contains("mac")) return Os.MAC;
31:         return Os.LINUX;
32:     }
33: 
34:     public static Arch detectArch() {
35:         String raw = System.getProperty("os.arch").toLowerCase();
36:         if (raw.contains("aarch64") || raw.contains("arm64")) return Arch.AARCH64;
37:         return Arch.X64;
38:     }
39: 
40:     /**
41:      * Returns the project-specific JDK home.
42:      *
43:      * Checks in order:
44:      *   1. TFOCR_JAVA_HOME environment variable (set by run.sh/bootstrap.sh)
45:      *   2. jdk/ directory in the project root (project-local install)
46:      *   3. The JVM that is running this code (java.home system property)
47:      */
48:     public static String getProjectJavaHome() {
49:         String env = System.getenv("TFOCR_JAVA_HOME");
50:         if (env != null && !env.isEmpty()) return env;
51:         File projectJdk = new File("jdk");
52:         if (projectJdk.isDirectory() && new File(projectJdk, "bin/java").canExecute()) {
53:             return projectJdk.getAbsolutePath();
54:         }
55:         return System.getProperty("java.home");
56:     }
57: }

(End of file - total 57 lines)
</content>
```

<path>/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/main/java/com/trulyfreeocr/util/SubprocessRunner.java</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: package com.trulyfreeocr.util;
2: 
3: import java.io.BufferedReader;
4: import java.io.File;
5: import java.io.IOException;
6: import java.io.InputStreamReader;
7: import java.util.ArrayList;
8: import java.util.List;
9: import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
10: 
11: /**
12:  * Utility for running external processes and capturing stdout/stderr.
13:  *
14:  * Two convenience modes:
15:  *   run(executable, args...)      — blocks until completion (no timeout).
16:  *   run(executable, args, ms)     — kills the process after <ms> milliseconds.
17:  *
18:  * Stderr is NOT merged with stdout (redirectErrorStream = false) so
19:  * callers can distinguish normal output from error diagnostics.
20:  */
21: public class SubprocessRunner {
22: 
23:     /**
24:      * Executes a command with no timeout.
25:      *
26:      * @param executable  The binary to run.
27:      * @param args        Variable-length argument list.
28:      * @return Result containing exit code, stdout, and stderr.
29:      */
30:     public static Result run(File executable, String... args) throws IOException {
31:         return run(executable, List.of(args), -1);
32:     }
33: 
34:     /**
35:      * Executes a command with an optional timeout.
36:      *
37:      * @param executable  The binary to run.
38:      * @param args        Argument list.
39:      * @param timeoutMs   Max wall-clock time in milliseconds (&le;0 = no timeout).
40:      * @return Result containing exit code, stdout, and stderr.
41:      */
42:     public static Result run(File executable, List<String> args, long timeoutMs) throws IOException {
43:         List<String> command = new ArrayList<>();
44:         command.add(executable.getAbsolutePath());
45:         command.addAll(args);
46: 
47:         ProcessBuilder pb = new ProcessBuilder(command);
48:         pb.redirectErrorStream(false);
49: 
50:         Process process = pb.start();
51: 
52:         if (timeoutMs > 0) {
53:             try {
54:                 boolean finished = process.waitFor(timeoutMs, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
55:                 if (!finished) {
56:                     process.destroyForcibly();
57:                     throw new IOException("Process timed out after " + timeoutMs + "ms: " + executable.getName());
58:                 }
59:             } catch (InterruptedException e) {
60:                 process.destroyForcibly();
61:                 Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
62:                 throw new IOException("Process was interrupted", e);
63:             }
64:         } else {
65:             try {
66:                 process.waitFor();
67:             } catch (InterruptedException e) {
68:                 process.destroyForcibly();
69:                 Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
70:                 throw new IOException("Process was interrupted", e);
71:             }
72:         }
73: 
74:         byte[] stdout = process.getInputStream().readAllBytes();
75:         byte[] stderr = process.getErrorStream().readAllBytes();
76:         int exitCode = process.exitValue();
77: 
78:         return new Result(exitCode, stdout, stderr);
79:     }
80: 
81:     /**
82:      * Holds the subprocess output.
83:      *
84:      * exitCode  Process exit status (0 = success).
85:      * stdout    Raw bytes written to standard output.
86:      * stderr    Raw bytes written to standard error.
87:      */
88:     public static class Result {
89:         private final int exitCode;
90:         private final byte[] stdout;
91:         private final byte[] stderr;
92: 
93:         public Result(int exitCode, byte[] stdout, byte[] stderr) {
94:             this.exitCode = exitCode;
95:             this.stdout = stdout;
96:             this.stderr = stderr;
97:         }
98: 
99:         public int getExitCode() { return exitCode; }
100:         public byte[] getStdout() { return stdout; }
101:         public byte[] getStderr() { return stderr; }
102:         public String getStdoutString() { return new String(stdout); }
103:         public String getStderrString() { return new String(stderr); }
104:     }
105: }

(End of file - total 105 lines)
</content>

9: /**

11:  * a single cleanup() call to delete them all.
12:  *
13:  * Each file is also registered with deleteOnExit() as a safety net
14:  * in case cleanup() is not called (e.g., JVM crash).
15:  */
16: public class TempFileManager {
17: 
18:     private final List<File> tempFiles = new ArrayList<>();
19: 
20:     /**
21:      * Creates a temp file and registers it for cleanup.
22:      *
23:      * @param prefix  File name prefix (e.g. "tfocr-").
24:      * @param suffix  File name suffix (e.g. ".png").
25:      * @return The created temporary File.
26:      */
27:     public File createTempFile(String prefix, String suffix) throws IOException {
28:         File f = Files.createTempFile(prefix, suffix).toFile();
29:         f.deleteOnExit();
30:         tempFiles.add(f);
31:         return f;
32:     }
33: 
34:     /**
35:      * Deletes all tracked temp files and clears the internal list.
36:      */
37:     public void cleanup() {
38:         for (File f : tempFiles) {
39:             if (f.exists()) f.delete();
40:         }
41:         tempFiles.clear();
42:     }
43: }

### Tool: read

  "filePath": "/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/README.md"
}
```

**Output:**

```
<path>/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: # TrulyFreeOCR
2: 
3: Commercially-safe OCR pipeline for non-searchable PDFs. All dependencies use permissive open-source licenses (Apache 2.0 / MIT / BSD) — no AGPL, no proprietary components.
4: 
5: **Input**: PDF with non-searchable pages (image-only scans)  
6: **Output**: Searchable, compressed PDF
7: 
8: ---
9: 
10: ## Pipeline
11: 
12: ```
13: Input PDF
14:     |
15:     v
16: PageExtractor  — PDFBox PDFRenderer (configurable DPI) → per-page BufferedImage
17:     |
18:     v
19: ImageSegmenter — Pure-Java foreground/background segmentation:
20:                    grayscale → background normalize → Otsu binarize → inpaint
21:     |
22:     +----+----+
23:     |         |
24:     v         v
25: JBIG2Comp.   OCREngine      (parallel)
26:     |         |
27:     | jbig2enc| Tesseract CLI
28:     | subproc | word-level bboxes with TSV output
29:     |         |
30:     +----+----+
31:     |
32:     v
33: PDFAssembler — Background layer + CCITT G4 foreground mask stencil
34:     |            + invisible OCR text (rendering mode 3)
35:     v
36: Output PDF (searchable, compressed)
37: ```
38: 
39: ---
40: 
41: ## Implemented Components
42: 
43: ### PageExtractor
44: Renders each PDF page via PDFBox's `PDFRenderer.renderImageWithDPI()`. Default DPI is 300, configurable via `settings.jsonc` or `--dpi` CLI flag.
45: 
46: ### ImageSegmenter
47: Pure-Java page segmentation (no Leptonica dependency). Four sub-steps:
48: 
49: 1. **Grayscale conversion** — ITU-R BT.601 luma formula: `Y = 0.299R + 0.587G + 0.114B`  
50:    Perception-weighted coefficients matching human visual sensitivity (most sensitive to green, least to blue).
51: 
52: 2. **Background normalization** — Corrects non-uniform illumination (shadows, scanner vignetting).
53:    - Divides the image into tiles (configurable via `segmenter.tileSize`, default 64×64 px)
54:    - Estimates background level per tile using a configurable percentile (default 95th) of pixel intensities
55:    - Builds a smooth background surface via **bilinear interpolation** between tile centres
56:    - Stretches each pixel: `new = old × 255 / bg_estimate` (background pixels map to white, text stays dark)
57: 
58: 3. **Otsu binarization** — Automatically finds the optimal threshold by maximising **inter-class variance**:
59:    `σ² = wB × wF × (μB − μF)²` where `w` = class weight and `μ` = class mean.
60:    Exhaustively searches all 256 grayscale levels for the split with the best separation.
61: 
62: 4. **Inpainting** — Replaces foreground (text) pixels with the nearest background pixel colour within a configurable radius (default 3 px). Produces a cleaned background layer for PDF re-assembly.
63: 
64: ### OCREngine
65: Runs Tesseract as a **subprocess** (not JNA/Tess4J) to avoid native-library version mismatches with system Leptonica.
66: 
67: - Input: BufferedImage → temp PNG
68: - CLI flags: `tesseract input.png output -l eng --psm 1 tsv` (language and PSM configurable)
69: - Output: TSV file parsed for **word-level** bounding boxes (`level=5` rows with `left, top, width, height, conf, text`)
70: - Each word returned as a `TextBlock` with bounding box and confidence score
71: 
72: ### JBIG2Compressor
73: Attempts compression via **jbig2enc** subprocess (flags configurable via `jbig2enc.flags`, default `-p -s`).
74: 
75: - jbig2enc outputs a `.sym` file (global symbol dictionary) and a `.jbig2` file (page data), concatenated for PDF JBIG2Decode streams
76: - Falls back to **CCITT Group 4** fax encoding via PDFBox's `CCITTFactory` when jbig2enc is unavailable
77: 
78: ### PDFAssembler
79: Re-assembles the output PDF using PDFBox with an MRC-like layer structure:
80: 
81: - **Layer 1 (background)**: Cleaned page image embedded via `LosslessFactory.createFromImage()`
82: - **Layer 2 (foreground stencil)**: Binary mask compressed as CCITT G4 `ImageMask` — reproduces text pixels at full sharpness on top of the cleaned background
83: - **Layer 3 (text)**: OCR words at their bounding-box positions, rendered in **mode 3 (NEITHER)** — invisible on screen/print, but selectable and searchable
84: - Uses a configurable Standard 14 font (default Helvetica) — no embedding needed
85: - **Coordinate transform**: `scaleX = pageWidth_pts / imageWidth_px`, Y-flip because image origin is top-left and PDF origin is bottom-left
86: 
87: ### MetadataPreserver
88: Copies document metadata from the source PDF to the output:
89: - **Document information** — title, author, subject, keywords, creator, producer
90: - **Outlines** (bookmark tree) — COS-level deep copy
91: - **Per-page annotations** — text notes, highlights, links (each annotation COS dictionary is cloned)
92: - **XML metadata** (XMP stream)
93: 
94: ---
95: 
96: ## Configuration
97: 
98: All pipeline parameters are configurable via `settings.jsonc` in the project root directory (JSON with `//` and `/* */` comments). CLI flags override file settings, which override hardcoded defaults.
99: 
100: | Setting | Default | Description |
101: |---|---|---|
102: | `native.dir` | `./native` | Native binaries directory (jbig2enc, etc.) |
103: | `tessdata.dir` | `./tessdata` | Tesseract language data directory |
104: | `tesseract.path` | `./native/linux/tesseract` | Tesseract executable (project-local wrapper) |
105: | `tesseract.language` | `eng` | Tesseract language model |
106: | `tesseract.psm` | `1` | Page segmentation mode |
107: | `rendering.dpi` | `300` | PDF rendering resolution |
108: | `segmenter.tileSize` | `64` | Background normalization tile size (px) |
109: | `segmenter.percentile` | `0.95` | Background level percentile per tile |
110: | `segmenter.inpaintRadius` | `3` | Inpainting search radius (px) |
111: | `jbig2enc.flags` | `-p -s` | Flags passed to jbig2enc |
112: | `pdf.font` | `HELVETICA` | Standard 14 font for OCR text |
113: | `pdf.minFontSize` | `1` | Minimum OCR text font size (pt) |
114: | `output.file` | `output.pdf` | Default output file path |
115: 
116: CLI flags that override corresponding settings: `--dpi`, `--language`, `--psm`, `--native-dir`, `--tessdata-dir`, `-o`/`--output`, `--settings` (path to a custom settings file).
117: 
118: To use a custom settings file path:
119: ```bash
120: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar --settings /path/to/custom.jsonc input.pdf
121: ```
122: 
123: ---
124: 
125: ## Building
126: 
127: ```bash
128: # Build the fat JAR
129: ./gradlew build
130: 
131: # Run all tests
132: ./gradlew test
133: ```
134: 
135: Requires a **Java 21+** JDK (project-local `jdk/` or `TFOCR_JAVA_HOME`).
136: 
137: ## Testing
138: 
139: Tests use generated sample PDFs in `tests/test-files/`:
140: - `blank.pdf` — single blank US Letter page
141: - `simple-text.pdf` — one page with lorem ipsum text
142: - `multi-page.pdf` — three-page document with distinct content per page
143: - `two-column.pdf` — two-column layout
144: - `with-annotations.pdf` — bookmarks, links, and comments
145: - `noisy-scan.pdf` — simulated scanner noise and skew
146: 
147: Regenerate test PDFs with:
148: ```bash
149: ./gradlew generateTestPdfs
150: ```
151: 
152: See [`Evaluation.md`](Evaluation.md) for the OCR accuracy evaluation plan —
153: WER/CER targets, parameter sensitivity sweeps, and performance baselines.
154: 
155: ## Current Status
156: 
157: | Phase | Component | Status |
158: |-------|-----------|--------|
159: | 1 | Gradle scaffold + CLI | Done |
160: | 2 | PageExtractor | Done |
161: | 3 | OCREngine | Done |
162: | 4 | ImageSegmenter | Done |
163: | 5 | PDFAssembler (basic) | Done |
164: | 6 | JBIG2Compressor + SubprocessRunner | Done |
165: | 7 | PDFAssembler JBIG2 integration | Done |
166: | 8 | MetadataPreserver | Done |
167: | 9 | bootstrap scripts | Done |
168: | 10 | Integration tests | Done |
169: 
170: ## Dependencies
171: 
172: ### Build & Runtime (from Gradle)
173: 
174: | Dependency | Version | License | Project |

Here are the complete findings:

---

## OCR Engine: Tesseract CLI via Subprocess (NOT Tess4J)

The project **uses the Tesseract command-line executable directly** as a subprocess. It explicitly **rejected Tess4J/JNA** due to native-library version mismatch issues with system Leptonica.

### Key Evidence

**File:** `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/main/java/com/trulyfreeocr/pipeline/OCREngine.java` (lines 19-25):
```java
/**
 * OCR engine that delegates to the Tesseract CLI via subprocess.
 *
 * Tess4J's JNA binding was originally planned, but lept4j's
 * Leptonica version requires symbols not present in the system's
 * liblept.so.5.  Running tesseract as a subprocess (with TSV output)
 * avoids this native-library version mismatch entirely and is more
 * portable across Linux distributions.
 */
```

**How it works (OCREngine.java, lines 86-95):**
1. Converts `BufferedImage` to grayscale (8-bit gray for ~100x speedup)
2. Writes image to a temporary PNG file
3. Spawns a subprocess: `tesseract <input.png> <output_prefix> -l eng --psm 1 tsv`
4. Sets `TESSDATA_PREFIX` environment variable to point to the bundled tessdata directory
5. Parses the resulting TSV output for word-level bounding boxes (level=5 rows)
6. Returns `PageResult` objects with word bounding boxes and confidence scores

**Default paths used (OCREngine.java, line 47):**
- Tesseract binary: `native/linux/tesseract`
- Tessdata directory: `tessdata` (fallback: `TESSDATA_PREFIX` env var, then `/usr/share/tesseract-ocr/5/tessdata`)
- Language: `eng`
- PSM (Page Segmentation Mode): `1` (automatic with OSD)

---

## OCR-Related References in Java Source Files

All matches are in:
- `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/main/java/com/trulyfreeocr/pipeline/OCREngine.java` -- the sole OCR engine implementation
- `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/main/java/com/trulyfreeocr/pipeline/PDFAssembler.java` -- uses OCR results to embed invisible text layer
- `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/test/java/com/trulyfreeocr/eval/OcrAccuracyTest.java` -- end-to-end OCR accuracy evaluation
- `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/main/java/com/trulyfreeocr/pipeline/JBIG2Compressor.java` -- uses SubprocessRunner for jbig2enc

No Java source file references `Tess4J`, `tess4j`, or `lept4j` in active code -- they only appear in a comment in OCREngine.java explaining why they were **not** used.

---

## References in build.gradle.kts

**File:** `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/build.gradle.kts`

- Line 38: `environment("TESSDATA_PREFIX", "${project.projectDir}/tessdata")` (test task)
- Line 50: `environment("TESSDATA_PREFIX", "${project.projectDir}/tessdata")` (eval test task)

**There are NO Tesseract, Tess4J, or OCR Java library dependencies** in `build.gradle.kts`. The OCR engine relies entirely on a Tesseract CLI binary external to the Java build.

---

## Complete OCR-Related Dependencies and Licensing

| `info.picocli:picocli` | 4.7.6 | Apache 2.0 | Command-line interface |
| `info.picocli:picocli-codegen` | 4.7.6 | Apache 2.0 | CLI annotation processor |
| `org.junit.jupiter:junit-jupiter` | 5.11.4 | EPL 2.0 | Testing |
| `org.junit.platform:junit-platform-launcher` | - | EPL 2.0 | Testing |

### Native / Bundled Dependencies (installed by `bootstrap.sh`, gitignored)

| Dependency | Location | License | Role in OCR |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Tesseract OCR** | `native/linux/tesseract` + `native/linux/lib/libtesseract.so.5` | **Apache 2.0** | THE OCR ENGINE -- called as subprocess |
| **Leptonica** | `native/linux/lib/liblept.so.5` | **BSD 2-Clause** | Image processing library used by Tesseract |
| **English tessdata** | `tessdata/eng.traineddata` | **Apache 2.0** | Tesseract English language model |
| **jbig2enc** | `native/linux/jbig2enc` + `native/linux/lib/libjbig2enc.so.0` | **Apache 2.0** | JBIG2 compression of binary image masks (not OCR itself, but in OCR pipeline) |
| **OpenJDK 21 LTS** | `jdk/` | **GPL 2.0 + Classpath Exception** | Runtime |

### Third-party libraries mentioned in NOTICE.md (some not in current Gradle deps)

The `NOTICE.md` at `/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/NOTICE.md` lists these as attribution notices (some may be transitive or historical):

| Library | License | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| **Tess4J** | Apache 2.0 | Listed in NOTICE but **NOT used** (was originally planned, then rejected) |
| **JNA (Java Native Access)** | Apache 2.0 / LGPL 2.1 dual | Listed but **NOT used** (needed by Tess4J/lept4j) |
| **lept4j** | Apache 2.0 | Listed but **NOT used** (JNA bindings for Leptonica, rejected due to version mismatch) |
| **commons-io** | Apache 2.0 | May be transitive; not in `build.gradle.kts` |
| **jboss-vfs** | Apache 2.0 | May be transitive; not in `build.gradle.kts` |
| **jai-imageio-core** | BSD 3-Clause | Listed but not in current Gradle deps |
| **SLF4J API** | MIT | Listed but not in current Gradle deps |
| **Bouncy Castle (BCPKIX/BCUtil/BCProv)** | MIT-like | Listed but not in current Gradle deps |

---

## Summary

**OCR engine:** **Tesseract CLI** (executed as a subprocess)
**License:** **Apache 2.0**
**Version targeted:** Tesseract 5 (the default fallback tessdata path is `/usr/share/tesseract-ocr/5/tessdata`)
**Java integration approach:** No Java<->Tesseract binding library (no Tess4J, no JNA). OCREngine.java uses `ProcessBuilder` to invoke the `tesseract` binary, reads TSV output, and parses it manually. This was a deliberate architectural decision documented in the source code to avoid native library version conflicts with system Leptonica.

<details>
<summary>Thinking</summary>

Now I have a complete picture. Let me also check the NOTICE.md file to ensure it accurately reflects what's actually used.

The key concern is: **Tesseract installed via `apt-get`** on Linux. On the user's system, they have Tesseract installed via `apt-get`, which typically installs from distro packages. Tesseract itself is Apache 2.0, but it depends on Leptonica (BSD 2-Clause). These are both business-friendly.

However, there's a potential issue I should flag: the `bootstrap.sh` still has lines creating symlinks for Tess4J/lept4j JNA lookup (lines 90-107 and 119-135), even though Tess4J was rejected and is NOT used. Those symlinks are dead code.

Let me also think about whether there are any other issues:
- OpenJDK from Adoptium: GPL 2.0 with Classpath Exception - this is fine for commercial use
- Tesseract: Apache 2.0 ✓
- Leptonica: BSD 2-Clause ✓  
- jbig2enc: Apache 2.0 ✓
- All traineddata: Apache 2.0 ✓
- PDFBox: Apache 2.0 ✓
- picocli: Apache 2.0 ✓
- JUnit: EPL 2.0 ✓ (test only)
- Shadow plugin: Apache 2.0 ✓

One thing I notice: The `bootstrap.sh` installs `apt-get install -y tesseract-ocr libtesseract-dev libleptonica-dev`. The `-dev` packages are not needed for runtime - they're only needed if you're compiling against the libraries. The project uses Tesseract CLI via subprocess, not the dev libraries. The `-dev` packages could be removed.

Also, lines 90-107 of bootstrap.sh create native symlinks for Tess4J/lept4j JNA lookup, but Tess4J/lept4j are NOT used. This is leftover dead code.

Let me now check the settings.jsonc for any dependency-related configurations.

</details>

**NOTICE.md issues:**
The NOTICE.md lists several dependencies that are NOT actually used in the project:
1. **Tess4J** - Not used (switched to Tesseract CLI)
2. **JNA (Java Native Access)** - Not used (Tess4J dependency)
3. **commons-io** - Not directly in build.gradle.kts (may be transitively from PDFBox though)

70:           cd "$BUILD_DIR"

72:           cd jbig2enc
73:           ./configure && make
74:           cp jbig2enc "$NATIVE_DIR/"
75:         )
76:         rm -rf "$BUILD_DIR"
77:         echo "jbig2enc built to $NATIVE_DIR/jbig2enc"

79:         echo "WARNING: cmake/g++ not found. Please install build tools and re-run,"

81:       fi

97:

  "filePath": "/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/README.md"
}
```

**Output:**

```
<path>/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: # TrulyFreeOCR
2: 
3: Commercially-safe OCR pipeline for non-searchable PDFs. All dependencies use permissive open-source licenses (Apache 2.0 / MIT / BSD) — no AGPL, no proprietary components.
4: 
5: **Input**: PDF with non-searchable pages (image-only scans)  
6: **Output**: Searchable, compressed PDF
7: 
8: ---
9: 
10: ## Pipeline
11: 
12: ```
13: Input PDF
14:     |
15:     v
16: PageExtractor  — PDFBox PDFRenderer (configurable DPI) → per-page BufferedImage
17:     |
18:     v
19: ImageSegmenter — Pure-Java foreground/background segmentation:
20:                    grayscale → background normalize → Otsu binarize → inpaint
21:     |
22:     +----+----+
23:     |         |
24:     v         v
25: JBIG2Comp.   OCREngine      (parallel)
26:     |         |
27:     | jbig2enc| Tesseract CLI
28:     | subproc | word-level bboxes with TSV output
29:     |         |
30:     +----+----+
31:     |
32:     v
33: PDFAssembler — Background layer + CCITT G4 foreground mask stencil
34:     |            + invisible OCR text (rendering mode 3)
35:     v
36: Output PDF (searchable, compressed)
37: ```
38: 
39: ---
40: 
41: ## Implemented Components
42: 
43: ### PageExtractor
44: Renders each PDF page via PDFBox's `PDFRenderer.renderImageWithDPI()`. Default DPI is 300, configurable via `settings.jsonc` or `--dpi` CLI flag.
45: 
46: ### ImageSegmenter
47: Pure-Java page segmentation (no Leptonica dependency). Four sub-steps:
48: 
49: 1. **Grayscale conversion** — ITU-R BT.601 luma formula: `Y = 0.299R + 0.587G + 0.114B`  
50:    Perception-weighted coefficients matching human visual sensitivity (most sensitive to green, least to blue).
51: 
52: 2. **Background normalization** — Corrects non-uniform illumination (shadows, scanner vignetting).
53:    - Divides the image into tiles (configurable via `segmenter.tileSize`, default 64×64 px)
54:    - Estimates background level per tile using a configurable percentile (default 95th) of pixel intensities
55:    - Builds a smooth background surface via **bilinear interpolation** between tile centres
56:    - Stretches each pixel: `new = old × 255 / bg_estimate` (background pixels map to white, text stays dark)
57: 
58: 3. **Otsu binarization** — Automatically finds the optimal threshold by maximising **inter-class variance**:
59:    `σ² = wB × wF × (μB − μF)²` where `w` = class weight and `μ` = class mean.
60:    Exhaustively searches all 256 grayscale levels for the split with the best separation.
61: 
62: 4. **Inpainting** — Replaces foreground (text) pixels with the nearest background pixel colour within a configurable radius (default 3 px). Produces a cleaned background layer for PDF re-assembly.
63: 
64: ### OCREngine
65: Runs Tesseract as a **subprocess** (not JNA/Tess4J) to avoid native-library version mismatches with system Leptonica.
66: 
67: - Input: BufferedImage → temp PNG
68: - CLI flags: `tesseract input.png output -l eng --psm 1 tsv` (language and PSM configurable)
69: - Output: TSV file parsed for **word-level** bounding boxes (`level=5` rows with `left, top, width, height, conf, text`)
70: - Each word returned as a `TextBlock` with bounding box and confidence score
71: 
72: ### JBIG2Compressor
73: Attempts compression via **jbig2enc** subprocess (flags configurable via `jbig2enc.flags`, default `-p -s`).
74: 
75: - jbig2enc outputs a `.sym` file (global symbol dictionary) and a `.jbig2` file (page data), concatenated for PDF JBIG2Decode streams
76: - Falls back to **CCITT Group 4** fax encoding via PDFBox's `CCITTFactory` when jbig2enc is unavailable
77: 
78: ### PDFAssembler
79: Re-assembles the output PDF using PDFBox with an MRC-like layer structure:
80: 
81: - **Layer 1 (background)**: Cleaned page image embedded via `LosslessFactory.createFromImage()`
82: - **Layer 2 (foreground stencil)**: Binary mask compressed as CCITT G4 `ImageMask` — reproduces text pixels at full sharpness on top of the cleaned background
83: - **Layer 3 (text)**: OCR words at their bounding-box positions, rendered in **mode 3 (NEITHER)** — invisible on screen/print, but selectable and searchable
84: - Uses a configurable Standard 14 font (default Helvetica) — no embedding needed
85: - **Coordinate transform**: `scaleX = pageWidth_pts / imageWidth_px`, Y-flip because image origin is top-left and PDF origin is bottom-left
86: 
87: ### MetadataPreserver
88: Copies document metadata from the source PDF to the output:
89: - **Document information** — title, author, subject, keywords, creator, producer
90: - **Outlines** (bookmark tree) — COS-level deep copy
91: - **Per-page annotations** — text notes, highlights, links (each annotation COS dictionary is cloned)
92: - **XML metadata** (XMP stream)
93: 
94: ---
95: 
96: ## Configuration
97: 
98: All pipeline parameters are configurable via `settings.jsonc` in the project root directory (JSON with `//` and `/* */` comments). CLI flags override file settings, which override hardcoded defaults.
99: 
100: | Setting | Default | Description |
101: |---|---|---|
102: | `native.dir` | `./native` | Native binaries directory (jbig2enc, etc.) |
103: | `tessdata.dir` | `./tessdata` | Tesseract language data directory |
104: | `tesseract.path` | `./native/linux/tesseract` | Tesseract executable (project-local wrapper) |
105: | `tesseract.language` | `eng` | Tesseract language model |
106: | `tesseract.psm` | `1` | Page segmentation mode |
107: | `rendering.dpi` | `300` | PDF rendering resolution |
108: | `segmenter.tileSize` | `64` | Background normalization tile size (px) |
109: | `segmenter.percentile` | `0.95` | Background level percentile per tile |
110: | `segmenter.inpaintRadius` | `3` | Inpainting search radius (px) |
111: | `jbig2enc.flags` | `-p -s` | Flags passed to jbig2enc |
112: | `pdf.font` | `HELVETICA` | Standard 14 font for OCR text |
113: | `pdf.minFontSize` | `1` | Minimum OCR text font size (pt) |
114: | `output.file` | `output.pdf` | Default output file path |
115: 
116: CLI flags that override corresponding settings: `--dpi`, `--language`, `--psm`, `--native-dir`, `--tessdata-dir`, `-o`/`--output`, `--settings` (path to a custom settings file).
117: 
118: To use a custom settings file path:
119: ```bash
120: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar --settings /path/to/custom.jsonc input.pdf
121: ```
122: 
123: ---
124: 
125: ## Building
126: 
127: ```bash
128: # Build the fat JAR
129: ./gradlew build
130: 
131: # Run all tests
132: ./gradlew test
133: ```
134: 
135: Requires a **Java 21+** JDK (project-local `jdk/` or `TFOCR_JAVA_HOME`).
136: 
137: ## Testing
138: 
139: Tests use generated sample PDFs in `tests/test-files/`:
140: - `blank.pdf` — single blank US Letter page
141: - `simple-text.pdf` — one page with lorem ipsum text
142: - `multi-page.pdf` — three-page document with distinct content per page
143: - `two-column.pdf` — two-column layout
144: - `with-annotations.pdf` — bookmarks, links, and comments
145: - `noisy-scan.pdf` — simulated scanner noise and skew
146: 
147: Regenerate test PDFs with:
148: ```bash
149: ./gradlew generateTestPdfs
150: ```
151: 
152: See [`Evaluation.md`](Evaluation.md) for the OCR accuracy evaluation plan —
153: WER/CER targets, parameter sensitivity sweeps, and performance baselines.
154: 
155: ## Current Status
156: 
157: | Phase | Component | Status |
158: |-------|-----------|--------|
159: | 1 | Gradle scaffold + CLI | Done |
160: | 2 | PageExtractor | Done |
161: | 3 | OCREngine | Done |
162: | 4 | ImageSegmenter | Done |
163: | 5 | PDFAssembler (basic) | Done |
164: | 6 | JBIG2Compressor + SubprocessRunner | Done |
165: | 7 | PDFAssembler JBIG2 integration | Done |
166: | 8 | MetadataPreserver | Done |
167: | 9 | bootstrap scripts | Done |
168: | 10 | Integration tests | Done |
169: 
170: ## Dependencies
171: 
172: ### Build & Runtime (from Gradle)
173: 
174: | Dependency | Version | License | Project |
175: |---|---|---|---|
176: | PDFBox | 3.0.6 | Apache 2.0 | https://pdfbox.apache.org |
177: | picocli | 4.7.6 | Apache 2.0 | https://picocli.info |
178: | Shadow plugin | 8.1.1 | Apache 2.0 | https://github.com/johnrengelman/shadow |
179: 
180: ### Test (from Gradle)
181:

183: |---|---|---|---|
184: | JUnit Jupiter | 5.11.4 | EPL 2.0 | https://junit.org/junit5/ |
185: | JUnit Platform Launcher | 1.11.4 | EPL 2.0 | https://junit.org/junit5/ |
186: 
187: ### Native / Bundled
188: 
189: All native dependencies are installed in project subdirectories and gitignored.
190: The `bootstrap.sh` script handles setting them up from scratch.
191: 
192: | Dependency | Project Location | License | Project |
193: |---|---|---|---|
194: | OpenJDK 21 LTS | `jdk/` | GPL 2.0 + Classpath Exception | https://adoptium.net |
195: | Tesseract OCR | `native/linux/tesseract` → `tesseract.bin` + `native/linux/lib/libtesseract.so.5` | Apache 2.0 | https://github.com/tesseract-ocr/tesseract |
196: | Leptonica | `native/linux/lib/liblept.so.5` | BSD 2-Clause | https://github.com/DanBloomberg/leptonica |
197: | jbig2enc | `native/linux/jbig2enc` → `jbig2enc.bin` + `native/linux/lib/libjbig2enc.so.0` | Apache 2.0 | https://github.com/agl/jbig2enc |
198: | English tessdata | `tessdata/eng.traineddata` | Apache 2.0 | https://github.com/tesseract-ocr/tessdata |
199: | Gradle wrapper | `gradlew` + `gradle/wrapper/` | Apache 2.0 | https://gradle.org |
200: 
201: Binary wrappers in `native/linux/` set `LD_LIBRARY_PATH` to `native/linux/lib/` so
202: the project-local shared libraries are used instead of system-wide ones.
203: 
204: ## License
205:

123:     private void runPipeline(File inputFile, File outputFile,
124:                              PageExtractor extractor, ImageSegmenter segmenter,
125:                              OCREngine ocrEngine, JBIG2Compressor compressor,
126:                              PDFAssembler assembler, boolean useMrc) throws IOException {

154:             }

157:         } else {

160:             foregroundMasks = null;
161:         }

164:         System.out.println("  Running OCR...");
165:         List<PageResult> ocrResults = new ArrayList<>(pages.size());
166:         for (int i = 0; i < pages.size(); i++) {
167:             long ts = System.nanoTime();
168:             ocrResults.add(ocrEngine.ocr(pages.get(i)));
169:             double elapsed = (System.nanoTime() - ts) / 1e9;

175:         // Phase 4: Assemble searchable PDF with optional MRC foreground overlay
176:         System.out.println("  Assembling PDF...");
177:         try (var doc = assembler.assemble(inputFile, backgrounds, foregroundMasks, ocrResults)) {
178:             doc.save(outputFile);
179:         }
180:         long t5 = System.nanoTime();
181:         System.out.printf("    Assembly done in %.1fs%n", (t5 - t4) / 1e9);
182:     }

1: package com.trulyfreeocr.util;
2: 
3: import java.io.IOException;
4: import java.nio.file.Files;
5: import java.nio.file.Path;
6: import java.nio.file.Paths;
7: import java.util.HashMap;
8: import java.util.Map;
9: 
10: public class Settings {
11: 
12:     private static Settings instance;
13: 
14:     private final Map<String, String> values;
15: 
16:     private static final Path DEFAULT_PATH = Paths.get("settings.jsonc");
17: 
18:     // System property key for overriding the settings file location.
19:     private static final String PROP_KEY = "tfocr.settings";
20: 
21:     public Settings() {
22:         this.values = new HashMap<>();
23:     }
24: 
25:     public Settings(Map<String, String> values) {
26:         this.values = new HashMap<>(values);
27:     }
28: 
29:     /**
30:      * Loads settings from the default location (settings.jsonc in CWD),
31:      * or from the path specified by the "tfocr.settings" system property.
32:      * Does nothing if the file does not exist — all getters fall back to
33:      * their supplied defaults.
34:      */
35:     public static Settings load() {
36:         Settings s = new Settings();
37:         Path path = findPath();
38:         if (path != null && Files.exists(path)) {
39:             try {
40:                 String raw = Files.readString(path);
41:                 s.values.putAll(parseJsonc(raw));
42:             } catch (IOException e) {
43:                 // file missing or unreadable — use defaults
44:             }
45:         }
46:         instance = s;
47:         return s;
48:     }
49: 
50:     /**
51:      * Returns the singleton instance.  Must be preceded by a call to load().
52:      */
53:     public static Settings getInstance() {
54:         if (instance == null) {
55:             instance = new Settings();
56:         }
57:         return instance;
58:     }
59: 
60:     // ---- typed accessors with defaults ----
61: 
62:     public String getString(String key, String defaultValue) {
63:         return values.getOrDefault(key, defaultValue);
64:     }
65: 
66:     public int getInt(String key, int defaultValue) {
67:         String v = values.get(key);
68:         if (v == null) return defaultValue;
69:         try { return Integer.parseInt(v); } catch (NumberFormatException e) { return defaultValue; }
70:     }
71: 
72:     public double getDouble(String key, double defaultValue) {
73:         String v = values.get(key);
74:         if (v == null) return defaultValue;
75:         try { return Double.parseDouble(v); } catch (NumberFormatException e) { return defaultValue; }
76:     }
77: 
78:     public boolean getBoolean(String key, boolean defaultValue) {
79:         String v = values.get(key);
80:         if (v == null) return defaultValue;
81:         return "true".equalsIgnoreCase(v);
82:     }
83: 
84:     // ---- path resolution ----
85: 
86:     private static Path findPath() {
87:         String prop = System.getProperty(PROP_KEY);
88:         if (prop != null && !prop.isEmpty()) {
89:             return Paths.get(prop);
90:         }
91:         return DEFAULT_PATH;
92:     }
93: 
94:     // ---- minimal JSONC parser (flat objects only) ----
95: 
96:     static Map<String, String> parseJsonc(String raw) {
97:         String stripped = stripComments(raw);
98:         return parseJson(stripped);
99:     }
100: 
101:     private static String stripComments(String input) {
102:         StringBuilder out = new StringBuilder(input.length());
103:         int i = 0;
104:         while (i < input.length()) {
105:             if (i + 1 < input.length() && input.charAt(i) == '/' && input.charAt(i + 1) == '/') {
106:                 // line comment — skip to end of line
107:                 i += 2;
108:                 while (i < input.length() && input.charAt(i) != '\n') i++;
109:                 continue;
110:             }
111:             if (i + 1 < input.length() && input.charAt(i) == '/' && input.charAt(i + 1) == '*') {
112:                 // block comment — skip to */
113:                 i += 2;
114:                 while (i + 1 < input.length() && !(input.charAt(i) == '*' && input.charAt(i + 1) == '/')) i++;
115:                 i += 2; // skip */
116:                 continue;
117:             }
118:             out.append(input.charAt(i));
119:             i++;
120:         }
121:         return out.toString();
122:     }
123: 
124:     private static Map<String, String> parseJson(String input) {
125:         Map<String, String> result = new HashMap<>();
126:         int i = skipWhitespace(input, 0);
127:         if (i >= input.length() || input.charAt(i) != '{') return result;
128:         i = skipWhitespace(input, i + 1);
129: 
130:         while (i < input.length()) {
131:             if (input.charAt(i) == '}') break;
132:             if (input.charAt(i) == ',') { i = skipWhitespace(input, i + 1); continue; }
133: 
134:             // parse key
135:             if (input.charAt(i) != '"') break;
136:             int keyStart = i + 1;
137:             int keyEnd = findStringEnd(input, keyStart);
138:             if (keyEnd < 0) break;
139:             String key = input.substring(keyStart, keyEnd);
140:             i = skipWhitespace(input, keyEnd + 1);
141: 
142:             if (i >= input.length() || input.charAt(i) != ':') break;
143:             i = skipWhitespace(input, i + 1);
144: 
145:             // parse value
146:             if (i >= input.length()) break;
147:             char c = input.charAt(i);
148:             String value;
149:             if (c == '"') {
150:                 int valStart = i + 1;
151:                 int valEnd = findStringEnd(input, valStart);
152:                 if (valEnd < 0) break;
153:                 value = input.substring(valStart, valEnd);
154:                 i = skipWhitespace(input, valEnd + 1);
155:             } else if (c == 't' && input.startsWith("true", i)) {
156:                 value = "true";
157:                 i = skipWhitespace(input, i + 4);
158:             } else if (c == 'f' && input.startsWith("false", i)) {
159:                 value = "false";
160:                 i = skipWhitespace(input, i + 5);
161:             } else if (c == 'n' && input.startsWith("null", i)) {
162:                 value = "null";
163:                 i = skipWhitespace(input, i + 4);
164:             } else {
165:                 // number
166:                 int valEnd = i;
167:                 while (valEnd < input.length() && (Character.isDigit(input.charAt(valEnd))
168:                         || input.charAt(valEnd) == '.' || input.charAt(valEnd) == '-'
169:                         || input.charAt(valEnd) == '+' || input.charAt(valEnd) == 'e'
170:                         || input.charAt(valEnd) == 'E')) {
171:                     valEnd++;
172:                 }
173:                 if (valEnd == i) break;
174:                 value = input.substring(i, valEnd);
175:                 i = skipWhitespace(input, valEnd);
176:             }
177:             result.put(key, value);
178:         }
179:         return result;
180:     }
181: 
182:     private static int skipWhitespace(String s, int pos) {
183:         while (pos < s.length() && Character.isWhitespace(s.charAt(pos))) pos++;
184:         return pos;
185:     }
186: 
187:     private static int findStringEnd(String s, int start) {
188:         int i = start;
189:         while (i < s.length()) {
190:             char c = s.charAt(i);
191:             if (c == '\\') {
192:                 i += 2; // skip escaped char
193:             } else if (c == '"') {
194:                 return i;
195:             } else {
196:                 i++;
197:             }
198:         }
199:         return -1;
200:     }
201: }

4. Language: `--language fra`
5. PSM: `--psm 6`

<content>
1: # TrulyFreeOCR
2: 
3: Commercially-safe OCR pipeline for non-searchable PDFs. All dependencies use permissive open-source licenses (Apache 2.0 / MIT / BSD) — no AGPL, no proprietary components.
4: 
5: **Input**: PDF with non-searchable pages (image-only scans)  
6: **Output**: Searchable, compressed PDF
7: 
8: ---
9: 
10: ## Pipeline
11: 
12: ```
13: Input PDF
14:     |
15:     v
16: PageExtractor  — PDFBox PDFRenderer (configurable DPI) → per-page BufferedImage
17:     |
18:     v
19: ImageSegmenter — Pure-Java foreground/background segmentation:
20:                    grayscale → background normalize → Otsu binarize → inpaint
21:     |
22:     +----+----+
23:     |         |
24:     v         v
25: JBIG2Comp.   OCREngine      (parallel)
26:     |         |
27:     | jbig2enc| Tesseract CLI
28:     | subproc | word-level bboxes with TSV output
29:     |         |
30:     +----+----+
31:     |
32:     v
33: PDFAssembler — Background layer + CCITT G4 foreground mask stencil
34:     |            + invisible OCR text (rendering mode 3)
35:     v
36: Output PDF (searchable, compressed)
37: ```
38: 
39: ---
40: 
41: ## Building
42: 
43: ```bash
44: # Build the fat JAR
45: ./gradlew build
46: 
47: # Run all tests
48: ./gradlew test
49: ```
50: 
51: Requires a **Java 21+** JDK (project-local `jdk/` or `TFOCR_JAVA_HOME`).
52: 
53: ---
54: 
55: ## Usage
56: 
57: ```bash
58: # Minimal: process a PDF with default settings
59: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf
60: 
61: # Specify output path
62: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf -o output.pdf
63: 
64: # Use a different language (fra, spa, deu, chi_sim, chi_tra, jpn)
65: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf --language fra
66: 
67: # Adjust Tesseract page segmentation mode
68: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf --psm 6
69: 
70: # Lower DPI for faster processing (less accurate)
71: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf --dpi 200
72: 
73: # Disable MRC compression (faster assembly, larger output)
74: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf --no-mrc
75: 
76: # Custom native/tessdata directories
77: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf \
78:     --native-dir ./custom-native --tessdata-dir ./custom-tessdata
79: 
80: # Load settings from a custom file (overrides settings.jsonc)
81: java -jar build/libs/trulyfreeocr.jar input.pdf --settings /path/to/custom.jsonc
82: 
83: # Using the project-local JDK wrapper
84: TFOCR_JAVA_HOME=jdk/linux ./gradlew run --args="input.pdf -o output.pdf"
85: ```
86: 
87: CLI flags override `settings.jsonc` values, which override hardcoded defaults. Run with `--help` for all options. You can also use `./gradlew run --args="..."` with a project-local JDK set via `TFOCR_JAVA_HOME` or `jdk/`.
88: 
89: ---
90: 
91: ## Testing
92: 
93: Tests use generated sample PDFs in `tests/test-files/`:
94: - `blank.pdf` — single blank US Letter page
95: - `simple-text.pdf` — one page with lorem ipsum text
96: - `multi-page.pdf` — three-page document with distinct content per page
97: - `two-column.pdf` — two-column layout
98: - `with-annotations.pdf` — bookmarks, links, and comments
99: - `noisy-scan.pdf` — simulated scanner noise and skew
100: 
101: Regenerate test PDFs with:
102: ```bash
103: ./gradlew generateTestPdfs
104: ```
105: 
106: See [`Evaluation.md`](Evaluation.md) for the OCR accuracy evaluation plan —
107: WER/CER targets, parameter sensitivity sweeps, and performance baselines.
108: 
109: ---
110: 
111: ## Implemented Components
112: 
113: ### PageExtractor
114: Renders each PDF page via PDFBox's `PDFRenderer.renderImageWithDPI()`. Default DPI is 300, configurable via `settings.jsonc` or `--dpi` CLI flag.
115: 
116: ### ImageSegmenter
117: Pure-Java page segmentation (no Leptonica dependency). Four sub-steps:
118: 
119: 1. **Grayscale conversion** — ITU-R BT.601 luma formula: `Y = 0.299R + 0.587G + 0.114B`  
120:    Perception-weighted coefficients matching human visual sensitivity (most sensitive to green, least to blue).
121: 
122: 2. **Background normalization** — Corrects non-uniform illumination (shadows, scanner vignetting).
123:    - Divides the image into tiles (configurable via `segmenter.tileSize`, default 64×64 px)
124:    - Estimates background level per tile using a configurable percentile (default 95th) of pixel intensities
125:    - Builds a smooth background surface via **bilinear interpolation** between tile centres
126:    - Stretches each pixel: `new = old × 255 / bg_estimate` (background pixels map to white, text stays dark)
127: 
128: 3. **Otsu binarization** — Automatically finds the optimal threshold by maximising **inter-class variance**:
129:    `σ² = wB × wF × (μB − μF)²` where `w` = class weight and `μ` = class mean.
130:    Exhaustively searches all 256 grayscale levels for the split with the best separation.
131: 
132: 4. **Inpainting** — Replaces foreground (text) pixels with the nearest background pixel colour within a configurable radius (default 3 px). Produces a cleaned background layer for PDF re-assembly.
133: 
134: ### OCREngine
135: Runs Tesseract as a **subprocess** (not JNA/Tess4J) to avoid native-library version mismatches with system Leptonica.
136: 
137: - Input: BufferedImage → temp PNG
138: - CLI flags: `tesseract input.png output -l eng --psm 1 tsv` (language and PSM configurable)
139: - Output: TSV file parsed for **word-level** bounding boxes (`level=5` rows with `left, top, width, height, conf, text`)
140: - Each word returned as a `TextBlock` with bounding box and confidence score
141: 
142: ### JBIG2Compressor
143: Attempts compression via **jbig2enc** subprocess (flags configurable via `jbig2enc.flags`, default `-p -s`).
144: 
145: - jbig2enc outputs a `.sym` file (global symbol dictionary) and a `.jbig2` file (page data), concatenated for PDF JBIG2Decode streams
146: - Falls back to **CCITT Group 4** fax encoding via PDFBox's `CCITTFactory` when jbig2enc is unavailable
147: 
148: ### PDFAssembler
149: Re-assembles the output PDF using PDFBox with an MRC-like layer structure:
150: 
151: - **Layer 1 (background)**: Cleaned page image embedded via `LosslessFactory.createFromImage()`
152: - **Layer 2 (foreground stencil)**: Binary mask compressed as CCITT G4 `ImageMask` — reproduces text pixels at full sharpness on top of the cleaned background
153: - **Layer 3 (text)**: OCR words at their bounding-box positions, rendered in **mode 3 (NEITHER)** — invisible on screen/print, but selectable and searchable
154: - Uses a configurable Standard 14 font (default Helvetica) — no embedding needed
155: - **Coordinate transform**: `scaleX = pageWidth_pts / imageWidth_px`, Y-flip because image origin is top-left and PDF origin is bottom-left
156: 
157: ### MetadataPreserver
158: Copies document metadata from the source PDF to the output:
159: - **Document information** — title, author, subject, keywords, creator, producer
160: - **Outlines** (bookmark tree) — COS-level deep copy
161: - **Per-page annotations** — text notes, highlights, links (each annotation COS dictionary is cloned)
162: - **XML metadata** (XMP stream)
163: 
164: ---
165: 
166: ## Configuration
167: 
168: All pipeline parameters are configurable via `settings.jsonc` in the project root directory (JSON with `//` and `/* */` comments). CLI flags override file settings, which override hardcoded defaults.
169: 
170: | Setting | Default | Description |
171: |---|---|---|
172: | `native.dir` | `./native` | Native binaries directory (jbig2enc, etc.) |
173: | `tessdata.dir` | `./tessdata` | Tesseract language data directory |
174: | `tesseract.path` | `./native/linux/tesseract` | Tesseract executable (project-local wrapper) |
175: | `tesseract.language` | `eng` | Tesseract language model |
176: | `tesseract.psm` | `1` | Page segmentation mode |
177: | `rendering.dpi` | `300` | PDF rendering resolution |
178: | `segmenter.tileSize` | `64` | Background normalization tile size (px) |
179: | `segmenter.percentile` | `0.95` | Background level percentile per tile |
180: | `segmenter.inpaintRadius` | `3` | Inpainting search radius (px) |
181: | `jbig2enc.flags` | `-p -s` | Flags passed to jbig2enc |
182: | `pdf.font` | `HELVETICA` | Standard 14 font for OCR text |
183: | `pdf.minFontSize` | `1` | Minimum OCR text font size (pt) |
184: | `output.file` | `output.pdf` | Default output file path |
185: 
186: CLI flags that override corresponding settings: `--dpi`, `--language`, `--psm`, `--native-dir`, `--tessdata-dir`, `-o`/`--output`, `--settings` (path to a custom settings file).
187:

1: package com.trulyfreeocr.pipeline;
2: 
3: import java.awt.image.BufferedImage;
4: import java.io.File;
5: import java.io.IOException;
6: import java.util.ArrayList;
7: import java.util.List;
8: 
9: import org.apache.pdfbox.Loader;
10: import org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.PDDocument;
11: import org.apache.pdfbox.rendering.PDFRenderer;
12: 
13: /**
14:  * Renders each page of a PDF to a BufferedImage at 300 DPI
15:  * using PDFBox's PDFRenderer.
16:  *
17:  * 300 DPI is the standard scanning resolution for OCR:
18:  *   - US Letter (8.5"x11")  → 2550 × 3300 px
19:  *   - A4 (210×297 mm)        → 2480 × 3508 px
20:  *
21:  * The renderer uses PDFBox's built-in SFF (subpixel font finalizer)
22:  * for high-quality text rendering.
23:  *
24:  * Implements AutoCloseable so the underlying PDDocument is released.
25:  * Callers should use try-with-resources.
26:  */
27: public class PageExtractor implements AutoCloseable {
28: 
29:     private PDDocument document;
30:     private final float dpi;
31: 
32:     public PageExtractor() {
33:         this(300f);
34:     }
35: 
36:     public PageExtractor(float dpi) {
37:         this.dpi = dpi;
38:     }
39: 
40:     /**
41:      * Loads a PDF and renders every page.
42:      *
43:      * @param pdf  Input PDF file.
44:      * @return List of BufferedImages, one per page, at the configured DPI.
45:      */
46:     public List<BufferedImage> extractPages(File pdf) throws IOException {
47:         document = Loader.loadPDF(pdf);
48:         PDFRenderer renderer = new PDFRenderer(document);
49:         int pageCount = document.getNumberOfPages();
50:         List<BufferedImage> pages = new ArrayList<>(pageCount);
51:         for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {
52:             BufferedImage img = renderer.renderImageWithDPI(i, dpi);
53:             pages.add(img);
54:         }
55:         return pages;
56:     }
57: 
58:     @Override
59:     public void close() throws IOException {
60:         if (document != null) {
61:             document.close();
62:         }
63:     }
64: }

**Output:**

```
<path>/home/bgu/GitHub/msmarkgu/TrulyFreeOCR/src/main/java/com/trulyfreeocr/pipeline/OCREngine.java</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
30:  *
31:  * CLI flags used:
32:  *   -l eng    — English language model
33:  *   --psm 1   — Automatic page segmentation with OSD
34:  *   tsv       — Output format: TSV (word-level bounding boxes)
35:  *
36:  * The output PageResult always reports pageNumber=1 because each
37:  * call processes exactly one BufferedImage.
38:  */
39: public class OCREngine {
40: 
41:     private final File tessdataDir;
42:     private final String tesseractPath;
43:     private final String language;
44:     private final String psm;
45: 
46:     public OCREngine() {
47:         this("tessdata", "native/linux/tesseract", "eng", "1");
48:     }
49: 
50:     public OCREngine(String tessdataDir, String tesseractPath, String language, String psm) {
51:         this.tesseractPath = tesseractPath;
52:         this.language = language;
53:         this.psm = psm;
54: 
55:         if (tessdataDir != null && !tessdataDir.isEmpty()) {
56:             this.tessdataDir = new File(tessdataDir);
57:         } else {
58:             String env = System.getenv("TESSDATA_PREFIX");
59:             if (env != null && !env.isEmpty()) {
60:                 this.tessdataDir = new File(env);
61:             } else {
62:                 this.tessdataDir = new File("/usr/share/tesseract-ocr/5/tessdata");
63:             }
64:         }
65:     }
66: 
67:     public PageResult ocr(BufferedImage image) throws IOException {
68:         int width = image.getWidth();
69:         int height = image.getHeight();
70: 
71:         // Convert to grayscale — Tesseract processes 8-bit gray ~100x faster than 24-bit RGB
72:         if (image.getType() != BufferedImage.TYPE_BYTE_GRAY) {
73:             BufferedImage gray = new BufferedImage(width, height, BufferedImage.TYPE_BYTE_GRAY);
74:             Graphics2D g = gray.createGraphics();
75:             g.drawImage(image, 0, 0, null);
76:             g.dispose();
77:             image = gray;
78:         }
79: 
80:         // Write image to temp file
81:         File tempPng = File.createTempFile("tfocr-", ".png");
82:         tempPng.deleteOnExit();
83:         ImageIO.write(image, "png", tempPng);
84:

89:                     tesseractPath,
90:                     tempPng.getAbsolutePath(),

93:                     "--psm", psm,

97:             pb.redirectErrorStream(true);
98: 
99:             Process process = pb.start();
100:             try (BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(
101:                     new InputStreamReader(process.getInputStream()))) {
102:                 // Read and discard stdout (status messages go here)
103:                 while (reader.readLine() != null) { }
104:             }
105:             boolean exited = process.waitFor(30, java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit.SECONDS);
106:             if (!exited) {
107:                 process.destroyForcibly();
108:                 throw new IOException("Tesseract timed out after 30 seconds");
109:             }
110:             int exitCode = process.exitValue();
111:             if (exitCode != 0) {
112:                 throw new IOException("Tesseract exited with code " + exitCode);
113:             }
114: 
115:             // Parse TSV output
116:             File tsvFile = new File(prefix + ".tsv");
117:             if (!tsvFile.exists()) {
118:                 return new PageResult(1, width, height, List.of());
119:             }
120: 
121:             List<TextBlock> blocks = parseTsv(tsvFile);
122:             return new PageResult(1, width, height, blocks);
123: 
124:         } catch (InterruptedException e) {
125:             Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
126:             throw new IOException("Tesseract was interrupted", e);
127:         } finally {
128:             // Cleanup temp files
129:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");

15: /**
16:  * Compresses a binary foreground mask via jbig2enc subprocess,
17:  * falling back to CCITT Group 4 fax encoding via PDFBox when
18:  * the native binary is unavailable.
19:  *
20:  * jbig2enc flags:
21:  *   -p  — Produce a global symbol dictionary (shared across pages).
22:  *   -s  — Refine smearing to improve symbol matching.
23:  */
24: public class JBIG2Compressor {
25: 
26:     private final String nativeDir;
27: 
28:     public JBIG2Compressor() {
29:         this("native");
30:     }
31: 
32:     public JBIG2Compressor(String nativeDir) {
33:         this.nativeDir = nativeDir;
34:     }
35: 
36:     /**
37:      * Holds compressed foreground-mask data.
38:      *
39:      * isJbig2  true = JBIG2 format (from jbig2enc); false = CCITT G4 fallback.
40:      * data     The compressed byte stream.
41:      * width    Original mask width  in pixels.
42:      * height   Original mask height in pixels.
43:      */
44:     public static class CompressionResult {
45:         private final boolean isJbig2;
46:         private final byte[] data;
47:         private final int width;
48:         private final int height;
49: 
50:         public CompressionResult(byte[] data, int width, int height, boolean isJbig2) {
51:             this.data = data;
52:             this.width = width;
53:             this.height = height;
54:             this.isJbig2 = isJbig2;
55:         }
56: 
57:         public boolean isJbig2() { return isJbig2; }
58:         public byte[] getData() { return data; }
59:         public int getWidth() { return width; }
60:         public int getHeight() { return height; }
61:     }
62: 
63:     /**
64:      * Attempts JBIG2 compression via jbig2enc; falls back to CCITT G4 on failure.
65:      *
66:      * @param foregroundMask  Binary image (TYPE_BYTE_BINARY, black=foreground).
67:      * @return CompressionResult with either JBIG2 or CCITT G4 data.
68:      */
69:     public CompressionResult compress(BufferedImage foregroundMask) throws IOException {
70:         File jbig2enc = findJbig2enc();
71:         if (jbig2enc != null) {
72:             try {
73:                 return compressWithJbig2enc(jbig2enc, foregroundMask);
74:             } catch (IOException e) {
75:                 // jbig2enc failed → fall through to fallback
76:             }
77:         }
78:         return compressWithFallback(foregroundMask);
79:     }
80: 
81:     /**
82:      * Locates the jbig2enc binary for the current OS.
83:      *
84:      * Searches native/{os}/jbig2enc (or jbig2enc.exe on Windows).
85:      * The base path can be overridden via system property "tfocr.native.dir"
86:      * (defaults to "native").
87:      *
88:      * @return The executable File, or null if not found.
89:      */
90:     private File findJbig2enc() {
91:         Os os = PlatformUtils.detectOs();
92:         String dirName;
93:         switch (os) {
94:             case WINDOWS: dirName = "win"; break;
95:             case MAC: dirName = "mac"; break;
96:             default: dirName = "linux";
97:         }
98:         File exe = new File(nativeDir + "/" + dirName, os == Os.WINDOWS ? "jbig2enc.exe" : "jbig2enc");
99:         if (exe.canExecute()) return exe;
100:         return null;
101:     }
102: 
103:     /**
104:      * Runs jbig2enc and concatenates global sym + page jbig2 into one byte array.
105:      *
106:      * PDF JBIG2Decode streams require global segments (symbol dictionary)
107:      * followed by page data — exactly the .sym + .jbig2 layout that
108:      * jbig2enc produces.
109:      */
110:     private CompressionResult compressWithJbig2enc(File jbig2enc, BufferedImage mask) throws IOException {
111:         File tempPng = File.createTempFile("tfocr-jbig2-", ".png");
112:         tempPng.deleteOnExit();
113:         javax.imageio.ImageIO.write(mask, "png", tempPng);
114: 
115:         try {
116:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
117: 
118:             SubprocessRunner.Result result = SubprocessRunner.run(jbig2enc,
119:                     "-p", "-s", tempPng.getAbsolutePath());
120:             if (result.getExitCode() != 0) {
121:                 throw new IOException("jbig2enc failed: " + result.getStderrString());
122:             }
123: 
124:             File symFile = new File(prefix + ".sym");
125:             File jbig2File = new File(prefix + ".jbig2");
126: 
127:             byte[] symData = symFile.exists() ? java.nio.file.Files.readAllBytes(symFile.toPath()) : new byte[0];
128:             byte[] jbig2Data = jbig2File.exists() ? java.nio.file.Files.readAllBytes(jbig2File.toPath()) : new byte[0];
129: 
130:             byte[] combined = new byte[symData.length + jbig2Data.length];
131:             System.arraycopy(symData, 0, combined, 0, symData.length);
132:             System.arraycopy(jbig2Data, 0, combined, symData.length, jbig2Data.length);
133: 
134:             return new CompressionResult(combined, mask.getWidth(), mask.getHeight(), true);
135:         } finally {
136:             String prefix = tempPng.getAbsolutePath().replaceAll("\\.png$", "");
137:             for (String ext : new String[]{".png", ".sym", ".jbig2"}) {
138:                 File f = new File(prefix + ext);
139:                 if (f.exists()) f.delete();
140:             }
141:         }
142:     }
143: 
144:     /**
145:      * Fallback: encodes the mask as CCITT Group 4 fax using PDFBox's CCITTFactory.
146:      */
147:     private CompressionResult compressWithFallback(BufferedImage mask) throws IOException {
148:         // Create a throwaway PDDocument to use CCITTFactory
149:         try (PDDocument doc = new PDDocument()) {
150:             PDImageXObject ccitt = CCITTFactory.createFromImage(doc, mask);
151:             return new CompressionResult(extractStreamBytes(ccitt), mask.getWidth(), mask.getHeight(), false);
152:         }
153:     }
154: 
155:     private static byte[] extractStreamBytes(PDImageXObject image) throws IOException {
156:         try (java.io.InputStream is = image.createInputStream()) {
157:             return is.readAllBytes();
158:         }
159:     }
160: }

18:  * Copies metadata from a source PDF to an output PDF.

20:  * Preserved elements:
21:  *   - PDDocumentInformation (title, author, subject, keywords, creator, producer)
22:  *   - PDDocumentOutline (bookmark tree) — COS-level deep copy
23:  *   - Per-page PDAnnotation lists — each annotation COS dictionary is duplicated
24:  *   - XML metadata stream (XMP)
25:  *
26:  * Limitations:
27:  *   - Annotation page references (e.g. link destinations) are not remapped.
28:  *   - Named destinations are preserved but may reference missing pages.
29:  *   - Outline entries pointing to specific pages are kept but not remapped
30:  *     (the output pages are in the same order, so page-number-based links
31:  *     generally still work).
32:  */
33: public class MetadataPreserver {
34: 
35:     /**
36:      * Copies all metadata from source to output.
37:      *
38:      * @param source      The original PDF.
39:      * @param output      The newly assembled PDF.
40:      * @param outputPages Output pages indexed to match source pages.
41:      */
42:     public void preserve(PDDocument source, PDDocument output, List<PDPage> outputPages) throws IOException {
43:         copyDocumentInfo(source, output);
44:         copyOutline(source, output);
45:         copyAnnotations(source, outputPages);
46:         copyXmlMetadata(source, output);
47:     }
48: 
49:     private void copyDocumentInfo(PDDocument source, PDDocument output) {
50:         PDDocumentInformation info = source.getDocumentInformation();
51:         if (info != null) {
52:             PDDocumentInformation dest = new PDDocumentInformation();
53:             copyIfSet(info::getTitle, dest::setTitle);
54:             copyIfSet(info::getAuthor, dest::setAuthor);
55:             copyIfSet(info::getSubject, dest::setSubject);
56:             copyIfSet(info::getKeywords, dest::setKeywords);
57:             copyIfSet(info::getCreator, dest::setCreator);
58:             copyIfSet(info::getProducer, dest::setProducer);
59:             output.setDocumentInformation(dest);
60:         }
61:     }
62: 
63:     private void copyIfSet(ThrowingSupplier<String> getter, ThrowingConsumer<String> setter) {
64:         try {
65:             String val = getter.get();
66:             if (val != null) setter.accept(val);
67:         } catch (Exception e) {
68:             // skip
69:         }
70:     }
71: 
72:     @FunctionalInterface
73:     private interface ThrowingSupplier<T> {
74:         T get() throws Exception;
75:     }
76: 
77:     @FunctionalInterface
78:     private interface ThrowingConsumer<T> {
79:         void accept(T t) throws Exception;
80:     }
81: 
82:     private void copyOutline(PDDocument source, PDDocument output) throws IOException {
83:         PDDocumentOutline srcOutline = source.getDocumentCatalog().getDocumentOutline();
84:         if (srcOutline == null) return;
85: 
86:         // Deep-copy the outline COS dictionary tree
87:         COSDictionary srcDict = srcOutline.getCOSObject();
88:         COSDictionary dstDict = deepCopyCOSDictionary(srcDict);
89:         PDDocumentOutline dstOutline = new PDDocumentOutline(dstDict);
90:         output.getDocumentCatalog().setDocumentOutline(dstOutline);
91:     }
92: 
93:     private void copyAnnotations(PDDocument source, List<PDPage> outputPages) throws IOException {
94:         int pageCount = Math.min(source.getNumberOfPages(), outputPages.size());
95:         for (int i = 0; i < pageCount; i++) {
96:             PDPage srcPage = source.getPage(i);
97:             PDPage dstPage = outputPages.get(i);
98: 
99:             List<PDAnnotation> annotations = srcPage.getAnnotations();
100:             if (annotations.isEmpty()) continue;
101: 
102:             COSArray dstAnnots = new COSArray();
103:             for (PDAnnotation ann : annotations) {
104:                 COSDictionary cloned = deepCopyCOSDictionary(ann.getCOSObject());
105:                 dstAnnots.add(cloned);
106:             }
107:             dstPage.getCOSObject().setItem(COSName.ANNOTS, dstAnnots);
108:         }
109:     }
110: 
111:     private void copyXmlMetadata(PDDocument source, PDDocument output) throws IOException {
112:         PDMetadata srcMeta = source.getDocumentCatalog().getMetadata();
113:         if (srcMeta == null) return;
114: 
115:         try (var in = srcMeta.createInputStream()) {
116:             byte[] data = in.readAllBytes();
117:             PDMetadata dstMeta = new PDMetadata(output);
118:             dstMeta.importXMPMetadata(data);
119:             output.getDocumentCatalog().setMetadata(dstMeta);
120:         } catch (Exception e) {
121:             // Non-critical — skip XML metadata copy on failure
122:         }
123:     }
124: 
125:     private static COSDictionary deepCopyCOSDictionary(COSDictionary original) {
126:         COSDictionary copy = new COSDictionary();
127:         for (var entry : original.entrySet()) {
128:             COSName key = entry.getKey();
129:             var value = entry.getValue();
130:             if (value instanceof COSDictionary dict) {
131:                 copy.setItem(key, deepCopyCOSDictionary(dict));
132:             } else if (value instanceof COSArray arr) {
133:                 copy.setItem(key, deepCopyCOSArray(arr));
134:             } else {
135:                 copy.setItem(key, value);
136:             }
137:         }
138:         return copy;
139:     }
140: 
141:     private static COSArray deepCopyCOSArray(COSArray original) {
142:         COSArray copy = new COSArray();
143:         for (var value : original) {
144:             if (value instanceof COSDictionary dict) {
145:                 copy.add(deepCopyCOSDictionary(dict));
146:             } else if (value instanceof COSArray arr) {
147:                 copy.add(deepCopyCOSArray(arr));
148:             } else {
149:                 copy.add(value);
150:             }
151:         }
152:         return copy;
153:     }
154: }

- `tessdata.dir`: `./tessdata`
- `tesseract.path`: `./native/linux/tesseract`

And in OCREngine.java constructor default:
- tessdataDir: "tessdata" 
- tesseractPath: "native/linux/tesseract"

The README's config table shows defaults as:
- `tessdata.dir`: `./tessdata`
- `tesseract.path`: `./native/linux/tesseract`

These are the settings.jsonc defaults, not the OCREngine hardcoded defaults. But since settings.jsonc always takes precedence (loaded by Settings.load()), the effective defaults are from settings.jsonc. This is a minor inconsistency when settings.jsonc doesn't exist.

But actually, the README says "CLI flags override `settings.jsonc` values, which override hardcoded defaults." So the config table should ideally show the hardcoded defaults, not the settings.jsonc values. Or at least be consistent.

Let me also check whether `./tessdata` with the `./` prefix works correctly in Paths.get(). Actually, `./tessdata` is the same as `tessdata` so it doesn't matter functionally.

OK, let me now compile a final list of all inconsistencies I can find:

1. **PDFAssembler Layer 1 background encoding** (line 151): Says `LosslessFactory.createFromImage()` always, but it's JPEG for non-MRC, Lossless PNG for MRC.
   
2. **Configuration table missing `pipeline.mrc.enabled`** (line 170-184): The setting exists in code and settings.jsonc.

3. **CLI flags list missing `--no-mrc`** (line 186): Flags that override settings don't mention `--no-mrc`.

4. **JBIG2Compressor flags not actually configurable** (lines 143, 181): The README says flags are configurable via `jbig2enc.flags`, but JBIG2Compressor.java hardcodes `-p -s`.

5. **Gradle wrapper version missing**: The dependency table shows "Gradle wrapper" with no version number.

6. **Shadow plugin listed as runtime dependency** (line 213): Shadow plugin is a build-time only plugin, not a runtime dependency. It's in the "Build & Runtime (from Gradle)" section but should be separate.

Let me now fix all these issues.
